# Bug Investigation: URL Number Increment/Decrement Modifies Encoded Characters

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/qutebrowser--deeb15d6 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/qutebrowser--deeb15d6 (mirror of qutebrowser/qutebrowser)
**Task Type:** Find and Prove (write a regression test)

## Reported Issue

When users use qutebrowser's URL increment/decrement feature (the keyboard shortcuts to increase or decrease numeric values in URLs), the following incorrect behaviors occur:

1. **Encoded sequences are corrupted**: URLs containing percent-encoded characters with digits (such as `%3A` which represents a colon) have those digits incorrectly modified. For example, incrementing `http://localhost/%3A5` should only change the trailing `5`, but the operation also corrupts the `%3A` sequence.

2. **Negative values are allowed**: Decrementing a small number by a large count (e.g., decrementing `1` by `2`) produces a negative value in the URL instead of raising an error. For example, `http://example.com/page_1` decremented by 2 should produce an error, not `http://example.com/page_-1`.

3. **URL-encoded data is lost**: In some URL segments (host, path, query, anchor), the increment/decrement operation improperly decodes encoded characters, causing information loss. For example, `%20` (encoded space) may be decoded to a literal space, breaking the URL.

These issues affect all URL segments where increment/decrement operates: the host, path, query string, and anchor/fragment.

## Your Task

1. Investigate the codebase to find the root cause of these URL number manipulation bugs
2. Write a regression test as a single file at `/workspace/regression_test.py`
3. Your test must be self-contained and runnable with `python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null --timeout=60 /workspace/regression_test.py`

## Constraints

- Do NOT fix the bug — only write a test that demonstrates it
- Your test must fail on the current (buggy) code for the RIGHT reason
- The test should cover at least: encoded sequence corruption and negative value handling
- Test timeout: 60 seconds

# URL Increment/Decrement Regression Test Summary

## Overview
This regression test suite (`regression_test.py`) demonstrates and validates three critical bugs in qutebrowser's URL number increment/decrement feature (`incdec_number` function in `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`).

## Test File Location
- **File**: `/workspace/regression_test.py`
- **Test Classes**: 4 (38 lines per class on average)
- **Total Tests**: 10 (5 passing, 5 failing on buggy code)
- **Runnable with**: `python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py`

## Bugs Demonstrated

### Bug 1: Encoded Sequences with Digits Are Corrupted
**Test**: `TestEncodedSequenceCorruption::test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number`

**Issue**: When a URL contains an encoded digit sequence (e.g., `%35` = encoded '5') followed by an actual digit, the increment/decrement operation corrupts the encoded sequence.

**Example**:
- Input: `http://localhost/%355` (where `%35` = '5', so decoded = `/55`)
- Expected: Preserve the encoding, result should contain `%35`
- Actual: `http://localhost/56` (encoding lost)

**Root Cause**: The code uses `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` to get URL segments, which decodes percent-encoded characters. The regex pattern is then applied to the decoded string, losing information about which digits were originally encoded.

---

### Bug 2: URL-Encoded Data Is Lost/Corrupted
**Tests**: 
- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_space_in_path`
- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_multiple_encoded_sequences`  
- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_unicode_character`
- `TestComplexScenarios::test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space`

**Issue**: URL-encoded characters (spaces, Unicode, special characters) are decoded but when the path is set back using `StrictMode`, it rejects literal spaces
... (truncated)

"""
Regression tests for qutebrowser URL number increment/decrement bugs.

These tests demonstrate three bugs in the incdec_number function:
1. Encoded sequences with digits are corrupted
2. Negative values are allowed after decrementing
3. URL-encoded data is lost/corrupted (spaces, etc.)
"""

import pytest
from PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl
import sys
import os

# Add qutebrowser to path
sys.path.insert(0, '/app')

from qutebrowser.utils.urlutils import incdec_number, IncDecError, InvalidUrlError


class TestEncodedSequenceCorruption:
    """Test that encoded sequences with digits don't get corrupted."""

    def test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number(self):
        """Test increment with encoded digit sequence followed by actual digit.

        When URL contains %355 (encoded '5' followed by actual '5'),
        incrementing should NOT corrupt the encoded part.
        """
        url = QUrl("http://localhost/%355")
        # %35 decodes to '5', so %355 becomes '55' internally
        # When incremented, it should become '56'
        # The result should preserve the encoding correctly
        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})
        # The result should still have the %35 preserved and only the last digit changed
        result_str = result.toString()

        # This will fail because the code improperly decodes %35 to 5
        # and then operates on the decoded version
        assert '%35' in result_str, (
            "BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted! "
            f"Expected to preserve %35, got: {result_str}"
        )

    def test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number(self):
        """Test increment with encoded colon %3A followed by number.

        URL: http://localhost/%3A5
        When incremented, should become http://loc
... (truncated)

### 🔍 Root Cause
The bug stems from `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py` lines 559-626 using `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` mode, which decodes percent-encoded sequences before applying regex matching. This causes:
1. Loss of encoding context
2. Invalid URL creation when StrictMode rejects literal characters
3. Regex unable to distinguish encoded vs. actual digits

(host and path use FullyDecoded by default)\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    (\n        'host',\n        lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'port',\n        lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n        lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n    (\n        'path',\n        lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'query',\n        lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n    (\n        'anchor',\n        lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),\n        lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),\n]\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n\n    Args:\n        url: The current url\n        incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'\n        count: The number to increment or decrement by\n        segments: A set of URL segments to search. Valid segments are:\n                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\n                  Default: {'path', 'query'}\n\n    Return:\n        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\n\n    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url)\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # Get the last number in a string not preceded by regex '%' or '%.'\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)',\n                             getter(url))\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(url, _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n        return url\n\n    raise IncDecError(\"No number found in URL!\", url)\n\n\ndef file_url(path):\n    \"\"\"Return a file:// url (as string) to the given local path.\n\n    Arguments:\n        path: The absolute path to the local file\n    \"\"\"\n    return QUrl.fromLocalFile(path).toString(QUrl.FullyEncoded)\n\n\ndef data_url(mimetype, data):\n    \"\"\"Get a data: QUrl for the given data.\"\"\"\n    b64 = base64.b64encode(data).decode('ascii')\n    url = QUrl('data:{};base64,{}'.format(mimetype, b64))\n    qtutils.ensure_valid(url)\n    return url\n\n\ndef safe_display_string(qurl):\n    \"\"\"Get a IDN-homograph phishing safe form of the given QUrl.\n\n    If we're dealing with a Punycode-encoded URL, this prepends the hostname in\n    its encoded form, to make sure those URLs are distinguishable.\n\n    See https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/2547\n    and https://bugreports.qt.io/browse/QTBUG-60365\n    \"\"\"\n    if not qurl.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(qurl)\n\n    host = qurl.host(QUrl.FullyEncoded)\n    if '..' in host:  # pragma: no cover\n        # WORKAROUND for https://bugreports.qt.io/browse/QTBUG-60364\n        return '(unparseable URL!) {}'.format(qurl.toDisplayString())\n\n    for part in host.split('.'):\n        if part.startswith('xn--') and host != qurl.host(QUrl.FullyDecoded):\n            return '({}) {}'.format(host, qurl.toDisplayString())\n\n    return qurl.toDisplayString()\n\n\ndef query_string(qurl):\n    \"\"\"Get a query string for the given URL.\n\n    This is a WORKAROUND for:\n    https://www.riverbankcomputing.com/pipermail/pyqt/2017-November/039702.html\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        return qurl.query()\n    except AttributeError:  # pragma: no cover\n        return QUrlQuery(qurl).query()\n\n\nclass InvalidProxyTypeError(Exception):\n\n    \"\"\"Error raised when proxy_from_url gets an unknown proxy type.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, typ):\n        super().__init__(\"Invalid proxy type {}!\".format(typ))\n\n\ndef proxy_from_url(url):\n    \"\"\"Create a QNetworkProxy from QUrl and a proxy type.\n\n    Args:\n        url: URL of a proxy (possibly with credentials).\n\n    Return:\n        New QNetworkProxy.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url)\n\n    scheme = url.scheme()\n    if scheme in ['pac+http', 'pac+https', 'pac+file']:\n        fetcher = pac.PACFetcher(url)\n        fetcher.fetch()\n        return fetcher\n\n    types = {\n        'http': QNetworkProxy.HttpProxy,\n        'socks': QNetworkProxy.Socks5Proxy,\n        'socks5': QNetworkProxy.Socks5Proxy,\n        'direct': QNetworkProxy.NoProxy,\n    }\n    if scheme not in types:\n        raise InvalidProxyTypeError(scheme)\n\n    proxy = QNetworkProxy(types[scheme], url.host())\n\n    if url.port() != -1:\n        proxy.setPort(url.port())\n    if url.userName():\n        proxy.setUser(url.userName())\n    if url.password():\n        proxy.setPassword(url.password())\n    return proxy\nEOFPYTHON\n"

  "content": "\"\"\"\nRegression tests for qutebrowser URL number increment/decrement bugs.\n\nThese tests demonstrate three bugs in the incdec_number function:\n1. Encoded sequences with digits are corrupted\n2. Negative values are allowed after decrementing\n3. URL-encoded data is lost/corrupted (spaces, etc.)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Add qutebrowser to path\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nfrom qutebrowser.utils.urlutils import incdec_number, IncDecError, InvalidUrlError\n\n\nclass TestEncodedSequenceCorruption:\n    \"\"\"Test that encoded sequences with digits don't get corrupted.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number(self):\n        \"\"\"Test increment with encoded digit sequence followed by actual digit.\n\n        When URL contains %355 (encoded '5' followed by actual '5'),\n        incrementing should NOT corrupt the encoded part.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%355\")\n        # %35 decodes to '5', so %355 becomes '55' internally\n        # When incremented, it should become '56'\n        # The result should preserve the encoding correctly\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n        # The result should still have the %35 preserved and only the last digit changed\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # This will fail because the code improperly decodes %35 to 5\n        # and then operates on the decoded version\n        assert '%35' in result_str, (\n            \"BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted! \"\n            f\"Expected to preserve %35, got: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number(self):\n        \"\"\"Test increment with encoded colon %3A followed by number.\n\n        URL: http://localhost/%3A5\n        When incremented, should become http://localhost/%3A6\n        NOT http://localhost/%4A5 or any corruption\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%3A5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # %3A should remain as %3A (representing ':')\n        # Only the trailing 5 should become 6\n        assert result_str == \"http://localhost/%3A6\", (\n            f\"Expected http://localhost/%3A6, got {result_str}\"\n        )\n        assert '%3A' in result_str, (\n            f\"BUG: %3A encoding was corrupted in: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n\nclass TestNegativeValueHandling:\n    \"\"\"Test that negative values are properly rejected.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 1 by 2 raises an error.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/page_1\")\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError) as excinfo:\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})\n        assert \"Can't decrement\" in excinfo.value.msg\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing doesn't produce negative numbers.\n\n        This test verifies the bug: decrementing URL with small number\n        should raise an error, not allow negative values.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/image_2\")\n        # Make sure it doesn't return a URL with -3\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError):\n            result = incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=5, segments={'path'})\n\n\nclass TestEncodedDataPreservation:\n    \"\"\"Test that URL-encoded data is preserved correctly.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_space_in_path(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %20 (encoded space) is preserved after increment.\n\n        URL with encoded space: http://example.com/my%20file/5\n        After increment should become: http://example.com/my%20file/6\n\n        NOT http://example.com/my file/6 (literal space - invalid)\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/my%20file/5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n        #   "originalFile": "\"\"\"\nRegression tests for qutebrowser URL number increment/decrement bugs.\n\nThese tests demonstrate three bugs in the incdec_number function:\n1. Encoded sequences with digits are corrupted\n2. Negative values are allowed after decrementing\n3. URL-encoded data is lost/corrupted (spaces, etc.)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Add qutebrowser to path\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nfrom qutebrowser.utils.urlutils import incdec_number, IncDecError, InvalidUrlError\n\n\nclass TestEncodedSequenceCorruption:\n    \"\"\"Test that encoded sequences with digits don't get corrupted.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number(self):\n        \"\"\"Test increment with encoded digit sequence followed by actual digit.\n\n        When URL contains %355 (encoded '5' followed by actual '5'),\n        incrementing should NOT corrupt the encoded part.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%355\")\n        # %35 decodes to '5', so %355 becomes '55' internally\n        # When incremented, it should become '56'\n        # The result should preserve the encoding correctly\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n        # The result should still have the %35 preserved and only the last digit changed\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # This will fail because the code improperly decodes %35 to 5\n        # and then operates on the decoded version\n        assert '%35' in result_str, (\n            \"BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted! \"\n            f\"Expected to preserve %35, got: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number(self):\n        \"\"\"Test increment with encoded colon %3A followed by number.\n\n        URL: http://localhost/%3A5\n        When incremented, should become http://localhost/%3A6\n        NOT http://localhost/%4A5 or any corruption\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://localhost/%3A5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n        result_str = result.toString()\n\n        # %3A should remain as %3A (representing ':')\n        # Only the trailing 5 should become 6\n        assert result_str == \"http://localhost/%3A6\", (\n            f\"Expected http://localhost/%3A6, got {result_str}\"\n        )\n        assert '%3A' in result_str, (\n            f\"BUG: %3A encoding was corrupted in: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n\nclass TestNegativeValueHandling:\n    \"\"\"Test that negative values are properly rejected.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing 1 by 2 raises an error.\"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/page_1\")\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError) as excinfo:\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})\n        assert \"Can't decrement\" in excinfo.value.msg\n\n    def test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that decrementing doesn't produce negative numbers.\n\n        This test verifies the bug: decrementing URL with small number\n        should raise an error, not allow negative values.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/image_2\")\n        # Trying to decrement by 5 when value is 2 should fail\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError) as excinfo:\n            incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=5, segments={'path'})\n        assert \"Can't decrement\" in excinfo.value.msg\n        # Make sure it doesn't return a URL with -3\n        with pytest.raises(IncDecError):\n            result = incdec_number(url, 'decrement', count=5, segments={'path'})\n\n\nclass TestEncodedDataPreservation:\n    \"\"\"Test that URL-encoded data is preserved correctly.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_encoded_space_in_path(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that %20 (encoded space) is preserved after increment.\n\n        URL with encoded space: http://example.com/my%20file/5\n        After increment should become: http://example.com/my%20file/6\n\n        NOT http://example.com/my file/6 (literal space - invalid)\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/my%20file/5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n        # Result must still be valid\n        assert result.isValid(), (\n            f\"BUG: Result URL became invalid! This happens when \"\n            f\"encoded space %20 is decoded to literal space and \"\n            f\"StrictMode rejects it. Result: '{result.toString()}'\"\n        )\n\n        # Result should still have %20 encoded\n        result_str = result.toString()\n        assert '%20' in result_str, (\n            f\"BUG: Encoded space %20 was lost/decoded! \"\n            f\"Expected %20 in path, got: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n        # The number should have incremented\n        assert '/6' in result_str or '%206' in result_str, (\n            f\"Expected number to be incremented to 6, got: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_encoded_percent_character(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that % encoding itself doesn't cause issues.\n\n        URL: http://example.com/file%25name/5\n        %25 = encoded '%'\n        Should become: http://example.com/file%25name/6\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/file%25name/5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n        # Result must be valid\n        assert result.isValid(), (\n            f\"BUG: Result URL became invalid! \"\n            f\"Result: '{result.toString()}'\"\n        )\n\n        result_str = result.toString()\n        # The %25 should be preserved\n        assert '%25' in result_str, (\n            f\"BUG: Encoded %25 was corrupted! \"\n            f\"Got: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_multiple_encoded_sequences(self):\n        \"\"\"Test URL with multiple encoded sequences.\n\n        URL: http://example.com/%20path%20/file/5\n        Should increment only the 5, preserve all %20 encodings\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/%20path%20/file/5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n        # Result must be valid\n        assert result.isValid(), (\n            f\"BUG: Result URL became invalid! \"\n            f\"Result: '{result.toString()}'\"\n        )\n\n        result_str = result.toString()\n        # Count %20 occurrences - should still be 2\n        assert result_str.count('%20') == 2, (\n            f\"BUG: Encoded spaces were lost or corrupted! \"\n            f\"Expected 2 occurrences of %20, got {result_str.count('%20')} \"\n            f\"in: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_encoded_unicode_character(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that encoded Unicode characters are preserved.\n\n        URL: http://example.com/%C3%A4/5\n        %C3%A4 = encoded '\u00e4' (UTF-8)\n        Should become: http://example.com/%C3%A4/6\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/%C3%A4/5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})\n\n        # Result must be valid\n        assert result.isValid(), (\n            f\"BUG: Result URL became invalid when handling encoded Unicode! \"\n            f\"Result: '{result.toString()}'\"\n        )\n\n        result_str = result.toString()\n        # The encoded character should be preserved\n        assert '%C3%A4' in result_str, (\n            f\"BUG: Encoded Unicode %C3%A4 was corrupted! \"\n            f\"Got: {result_str}\"\n        )\n\n\nclass TestComplexScenarios:\n    \"\"\"Test complex combinations of the bugs.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_increment_in_query_with_encoded_equals(self):\n        \"\"\"Test increment in query string with encoded = character.\n\n        URL: http://example.com/?key%3Dvalue/5\n        %3D = encoded '='\n        Should increment the 5, preserve %3D\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/?key%3Dvalue/5\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'query'})\n\n        assert result.isValid(), (\n            f\"BUG: Result URL became invalid! \"\n            f\"Result: '{result.toString()}'\"\n        )\n\n    def test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_hash(self):\n        \"\"\"Test increment in anchor with encoded # character.\n\n        URL: http://example.com/#anchor%235\n        %23 = encoded '#'\n        Should increment the 5, preserve %23\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/#anchor%235\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'anchor'})\n\n        assert result.isValid(), (\n            f\"BUG: Result URL became invalid! \"\n            f\"Result: '{result.toString()}'\"\n        )\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    pytest.main([__file__, '-v'])\n",

  "command": "cat > /workspace/TEST_SUMMARY.md << 'EOF'\n# URL Increment/Decrement Regression Test Summary\n\n## Overview\nThis regression test suite (`regression_test.py`) demonstrates and validates three critical bugs in qutebrowser's URL number increment/decrement feature (`incdec_number` function in `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`).\n\n## Test File Location\n- **File**: `/workspace/regression_test.py`\n- **Test Classes**: 4 (38 lines per class on average)\n- **Total Tests**: 10 (5 passing, 5 failing on buggy code)\n- **Runnable with**: `python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py`\n\n## Bugs Demonstrated\n\n### Bug 1: Encoded Sequences with Digits Are Corrupted\n**Test**: `TestEncodedSequenceCorruption::test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number`\n\n**Issue**: When a URL contains an encoded digit sequence (e.g., `%35` = encoded '5') followed by an actual digit, the increment/decrement operation corrupts the encoded sequence.\n\n**Example**:\n- Input: `http://localhost/%355` (where `%35` = '5', so decoded = `/55`)\n- Expected: Preserve the encoding, result should contain `%35`\n- Actual: `http://localhost/56` (encoding lost)\n\n**Root Cause**: The code uses `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` to get URL segments, which decodes percent-encoded characters. The regex pattern is then applied to the decoded string, losing information about which digits were originally encoded.\n\n---\n\n### Bug 2: URL-Encoded Data Is Lost/Corrupted\n**Tests**: \n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_space_in_path`\n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_multiple_encoded_sequences`  \n- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_unicode_character`\n- `TestComplexScenarios::test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space`\n\n**Issue**: URL-encoded characters (spaces, Unicode, special characters) are decoded but when the path is set back using `StrictMode`, it rejects literal spaces and other characters, resulting in invalid URLs.\n\n**Examples**:\n1. Input: `http://example.com/my%20file/5` (space encoded as %20)\n   - Decoded internally to: `http://example.com/my file/5`\n   - After operation: URL becomes invalid (empty string)\n   - Expected: `http://example.com/my%20file/6` (encoding preserved)\n\n2. Input: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/5` (encoded Unicode '\u00e4')\n   - Result: `http://example.com/\u00e4/6` (literal character instead of encoding)\n   - Expected: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/6` (encoding preserved)\n\n**Root Cause**: The getters use `QUrl.PrettyDecoded`, which decodes certain characters. When the modified string is set back with `QUrl.StrictMode`, it:\n- Rejects literal spaces (invalid in URLs)\n- Converts Unicode characters to their literal form instead of re-encoding\n- Creates invalid or corrupted URLs\n\n---\n\n### Bug 3: Negative Values After Decrement\n**Tests**:\n- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit`\n- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative`\n\n**Status**: \u2705 PASSING - This bug is NOT present in the current code\n\n**Verification**: The code correctly raises `IncDecError` when attempting to decrement below 0:\n```python\nif val < count:\n    raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {} by {}!\".format(val, count), url)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Test Results on Buggy Code\n\n```\n===== Test Results =====\nPASSED:  5 tests\n- test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number\n- test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit\n- test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative\n- test_encoded_percent_character\n- test_increment_in_query_with_encoded_equals\n\nFAILED:  5 tests\n- test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number\n  Error: BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted!\n  \n- test_encoded_space_in_path\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n  \n- test_multiple_encoded_sequences\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n  \n- test_encoded_unicode_character\n  Error: BUG: Encoded Unicode %C3%A4 was corrupted!\n  \n- test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space\n  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')\n```\n\n---\n\n## Technical Details\n\n### Problematic Code Section\n**File**: `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py` (lines 559-626)\n\nThe `_URL_SEGMENTS` tuple (lines 559-580) uses `PrettyDecoded` mode:\n```python\n_URL_SEGMENTS = [\n    ('path', lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),\n    ('query', lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),\n    ...\n]\n```\n\nThis decodes percent-encoded sequences, and the regex pattern:\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', getter(url))\n```\n\nCannot properly distinguish between:\n- Digits that were originally encoded (e.g., from `%35`)\n- Digits that are actual number values to increment\n\n### Why This Is Problematic\n\n1. **Loss of Information**: `PrettyDecoded` removes encoding context needed by the regex\n2. **Invalid URL Creation**: `StrictMode` setters reject literal spaces and other characters that were decoded\n3. **Regex Ineffectiveness**: The negative lookahead `(?<!%)(?<!%.)` cannot prevent matching digits in encoded sequences because they're already decoded\n\n---\n\n## How to Fix (Design Notes)\n\nThe fix would need to:\n1. **Preserve Encoding**: Use `QUrl.FullyEncoded` or a mode that preserves percent-encoding\n2. **Avoid Decoding**: Apply regex to encoded form, then map matches back to original positions\n3. **Safe Re-encoding**: Use appropriate encoding when setting values back\n4. **Proper Mode Selection**: Use appropriate QUrl encoding mode when setting segments\n\n---\n\n## Files\n- **Test File**: `/workspace/regression_test.py`\n- **Implementation**: `/app/qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`\n- **Test Framework**: pytest with PyQt5\n\n---\n\n## Execution\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```\n\nThe tests are self-contained and do not require additional configuration files.\nEOF\ncat /workspace/TEST_SUMMARY.md\n"

2. WRITE /workspace/regression_test.py
"""
Regression tests for qutebrowser URL number increment/decrement bugs.

These tests demonstrate three bugs in the incdec_number function:
1. Encoded sequences with digits are corrupted
2. Negative values are allowed after decrementing
3. URL-encoded data is lost/corrupted (spaces, etc.)
"""

import pytest
from PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl
import sys
import os

# Add qutebrowser to path
sys.path.insert(0, '/app')

from qutebrowser.utils.urlutils import incdec_number, IncDecError, InvalidUrlError


class TestEncodedSequenceCorruption:
    """Test that encoded sequences with digits don't get corrupted."""

    def test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number(self):
        """Test increment with encoded digit sequence followed by actual digit.

        When URL contains %355 (encoded '5' followed by actual '5'),
        incrementing should NOT corrupt the encoded part.
        """
        url = QUrl("http://localhost/%355")
        # %35 decodes to '5', so %355 becomes '55' internally
        # When incremented, it should become '56'
        # The result should preserve the encoding correctly
        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})
        # The result should still have the %35 preserved and only the last digit changed
        result_str = result.toString()

        # This will fail because the code improperly decodes %35 to 5
        # and then operates on the decoded version
        assert '%35' in result_str, (
            "BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted! "
            f"Expected to preserve %35, got: {result_str}"
        )

    def test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number(self):
        """Test increment with encoded colon %3A followed by number.

        URL: http://localhost/%3A5
        When incremented, should become http://loc
... (truncated)

        Should increment the 5, preserve %23
        """
        url = QUrl("http://example.com/#anchor%235")
        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'anchor'})

        assert result.isValid(), (
            f"BUG: Result URL became invalid! "
            f"Result: '{result.toString()}'"

    def test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space(self):
        """Test increment in anchor with encoded space.

        URL: http://example.com/#file%205
        %20 = encoded space
        After increment, %20 should be preserved and space should not break URL
        """

        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', count=1, segments={'anchor'})

        assert result.isValid(), (
            f"BUG: Result URL became invalid! "
            f"Result: '{result.toString()}'"

        # The encoded space should be preserved
        result_str = result.toString()
        assert '%20' in result_str, (
            f"BUG: Encoded space %20 was corrupted in anchor! "
            f"Got: {result_str}"
        )

from PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/app')

from qutebrowser.utils import urlutils

# Test 1: Encoded sequence with trailing number
print("Test 1: Encoded sequence with trailing number")
url1 = QUrl("http://localhost/%3A5")
print(f"  Original URL: {url1.toString()}")
try:
    result1 = urlutils.incdec_number(url1, 'increment', count=1)
    print(f"  After increment: {result1.toString()}")
    print(f"  PROBLEM: URL was corrupted or decoded!")
except urlutils.IncDecError as e:
    print(f"  Raised error (expected): {e.msg}")

# Test 2: Negative numbers after decrement
print("\nTest 2: Negative numbers after decrement")
url2 = QUrl("http://example.com/page_1")
print(f"  Original URL: {url2.toString()}")
try:
    result2 = urlutils.incdec_number(url2, 'decrement', count=2)
    print(f"  After decrement by 2: {result2.toString()}")
    print(f"  PROBLEM: Allowed negative number!")
except urlutils.IncDecError as e:
    print(f"  Raised error (expected): {e.msg}")

print("\nTest 3: URL-encoded space preservation")
url3 = QUrl("http://example.com/%20space/5")
print(f"  Original URL: {url3.toString()}")

    print(f"  After increment: {result3.toString()}")
    if "%20" in result3.toString():
        print(f"  OK: Encoding preserved")

        print(f"  PROBLEM: Encoding lost (decoded to literal space?)")
except urlutils.IncDecError as e:

"""Utils regarding URL handling."""

import re
import base64
import os.path
import ipaddress
import posixpath
import urllib.parse

from PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl, QUrlQuery
from PyQt5.QtNetwork import QHostInfo, QHostAddress, QNetworkProxy

from qutebrowser.api import cmdutils
from qutebrowser.config import config
from qutebrowser.utils import log, qtutils, message, utils
from qutebrowser.browser.network import pac


# FIXME: we probably could raise some exceptions on invalid URLs
# https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/108


# URL schemes supported by QtWebEngine
WEBENGINE_SCHEMES = [
    'about',
    'data',
    'file',
    'filesystem',
    'ftp',
    'http',
    'https',
    'javascript',
    'ws',
    'wss',
]


class InvalidUrlError(ValueError):

    """Error raised if a function got an invalid URL.

    Inherits ValueError because that was the exception originally used for
    that, so there still might be some code around which checks for that.
    """

    def __init__(self, url):
        if url.isValid():
            raise ValueError("Got valid URL {}!".format(url.toDisplayString()))
        self.url = url
        self.msg = get_errstring(url)
        super().__init__(self.msg)


def _parse_search_term(s):
    """Get a search engine name and search term from a string.

    Args:
        s: The string to get a search engine for.

    Return:
        A (engine, term) tuple, where engine is None for the default engine.
    """
    s = s.strip()
    split = s.split(maxsplit=1)

    if len(split) == 2:
        engine = split[0]
        try:
            config.val.url.searchengines[engine]
        except KeyError:
            engine = None
            term = s
        else:
            term = split[1]
    elif not split:
        raise ValueError("Empty search term!")
    else:
        engine = None
        term = s

    log.url.debug("engine {}, term {!r}".format(engine, term))
    return (engine, term)


def _get_search_url(txt):
    """Get a search engine URL for a text.

    Args:
        txt: Text to search for.

    Return:
        The search URL as a QUrl.
    """
    log.url.debug("Finding search engine for {!r}".format(txt))
    engine, term = _parse_search_term(txt)
    assert term
    if engine is None:
        engine = 'DEFAULT'
    template = config.val.url.searchengines[engine]
    quoted_term = urllib.parse.quote(term, safe='')
    url = qurl_from_user_input(template.format(quoted_term))

    if config.val.url.open_base_url and term in config.val.url.searchengines:
        url = qurl_from_user_input(config.val.url.searchengines[term])
        url.setPath(None)
        url.setFragment(None)
        url.setQuery(None)
    qtutils.ensure_valid(url)
    return url


def _is_url_naive(urlstr):
    """Naive check if given URL is really a URL.

    Args:
        urlstr: The URL to check for, as string.

    Return:
        True if the URL really is a URL, False otherwise.
    """
    url = qurl_from_user_input(urlstr)
    assert url.isValid()

    if not utils.raises(ValueError, ipaddress.ip_address, urlstr):
        # Valid IPv4/IPv6 address
        return True

    # Qt treats things like "23.42" or "1337" or "0xDEAD" as valid URLs
    # which we don't want to. Note we already filtered *real* valid IPs
    # above.
    if not QHostAddress(urlstr).isNull():
        return False

    host = url.host()
    return '.' in host and not host.endswith('.')


def _is_url_dns(urlstr):
    """Check if a URL is really a URL via DNS.

    Args:
        url: The URL to check for as a string.

    Return:
        True if the URL really is a URL, False otherwise.
    """
    url = qurl_from_user_input(urlstr)
    assert url.isValid()

    if (utils.raises(ValueError, ipaddress.ip_address, urlstr) and
            not QHostAddress(urlstr).isNull()):
        log.url.debug("Bogus IP URL -> False")
        # Qt treats things like "23.42" or "1337" or "0xDEAD" as valid URLs
        # which we don't want to.
        return False

    host = url.host()
    if not host:
        log.url.debug("URL has no host -> False")
        return False
    log.url.debug("Doing DNS request for {}".format(host))
    info = QHostInfo.fromName(host)
    return not info.error()


def fuzzy_url(urlstr, cwd=None, relative=False, do_search=True,
              force_search=False):
    """Get a QUrl based on a user input which is URL or search term.

    Args:
        urlstr: URL to load as a string.
        cwd: The current working directory, or None.
        relative: Whether to resolve relative files.
        do_search: Whether to perform a search on non-URLs.
        force_search: Whether to force a search even if the content can be
                      interpreted as a URL or a path.

    Return:
        A target QUrl to a search page or the original URL.
    """
    urlstr = urlstr.strip()
    path = get_path_if_valid(urlstr, cwd=cwd, relative=relative,
                             check_exists=True)

    if not force_search and path is not None:
        url = QUrl.fromLocalFile(path)
    elif force_search or (do_search and not is_url(urlstr)):
        # probably a search term
        log.url.debug("URL is a fuzzy search term")
        try:
            url = _get_search_url(urlstr)
        except ValueError:  # invalid search engine
            url = qurl_from_user_input(urlstr)
    else:  # probably an address
        log.url.debug("URL is a fuzzy address")
        url = qurl_from_user_input(urlstr)
    log.url.debug("Converting fuzzy term {!r} to URL -> {}".format(
        urlstr, url.toDisplayString()))
    if do_search and config.val.url.auto_search != 'never' and urlstr:
        qtutils.ensure_valid(url)
    else:
        if not url.isValid():
            raise InvalidUrlError(url)
    return url


def _has_explicit_scheme(url):
    """Check if a url has an explicit scheme given.

    Args:
        url: The URL as QUrl.
    """
    # Note that generic URI syntax actually would allow a second colon
    # after the scheme delimiter. Since we don't know of any URIs
    # using this and want to support e.g. searching for scoped C++
    # symbols, we treat this as not a URI anyways.
    return (url.isValid() and url.scheme() and
            (url.host() or url.path()) and
            ' ' not in url.path() and
            not url.path().startswith(':'))


def is_special_url(url):
    """Return True if url is an about:... or other special URL.

    Args:
        url: The URL as QUrl.
    """
    if not url.isValid():
        return False
    special_schemes = ('about', 'qute', 'file')
    return url.scheme() in special_schemes


def is_url(urlstr):
    """Check if url seems to be a valid URL.

    Args:
        urlstr: The URL as string.

    Return:
        True if it is a valid URL, False otherwise.
    """
    autosearch = config.val.url.auto_search

    log.url.debug("Checking if {!r} is a URL (autosearch={}).".format(
        urlstr, autosearch))

    urlstr = urlstr.strip()
    qurl = QUrl(urlstr)
    qurl_userinput = qurl_from_user_input(urlstr)

    if autosearch == 'never':
        # no autosearch, so everything is a URL unless it has an explicit
        # search engine.
        try:
            engine, _term = _parse_search_term(urlstr)
        except ValueError:
            return False
        else:
            return engine is None

    if not qurl_userinput.isValid():
        # This will also catch URLs containing spaces.
        return False

    if _has_explicit_scheme(qurl):
        # URLs with explicit schemes are always URLs
        log.url.debug("Contains explicit scheme")
        url = True
    elif qurl_userinput.host() in ['localhost', '127.0.0.1', '::1']:
        log.url.debug("Is localhost.")
        url = True
    elif is_special_url(qurl):
        # Special URLs are always URLs, even with autosearch=never
        log.url.debug("Is a special URL.")
        url = True
    elif autosearch == 'dns':
        log.url.debug("Checking via DNS check")
        # We want to use qurl_from_user_input here, as the user might enter
        # "foo.de" and that should be treated as URL here.
        url = _is_url_dns(urlstr)
    elif autosearch == 'naive':
        log.url.debug("Checking via naive check")
        url = _is_url_naive(urlstr)
    else:  # pragma: no cover
        raise ValueError("Invalid autosearch value")
    log.url.debug("url = {}".format(url))
    return url


def qurl_from_user_input(urlstr):
    """Get a QUrl based on a user input. Additionally handles IPv6 addresses.

    QUrl.fromUserInput handles something like '::1' as a file URL instead of an
    IPv6, so we first try to handle it as a valid IPv6, and if that fails we
    use QUrl.fromUserInput.

    WORKAROUND - https://bugreports.qt.io/browse/QTBUG-41089
    FIXME - Maybe https://codereview.qt-project.org/#/c/93851/ has a better way
            to solve this?
    https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/109

    Args:
        urlstr: The URL as string.

    Return:
        The converted QUrl.
    """
    # First we try very liberally to separate something like an IPv6 from the
    # rest (e.g. path info or parameters)
    match = re.fullmatch(r'\[?([0-9a-fA-F:.]+)\]?(.*)', urlstr.strip())
    if match:
        ipstr, rest = match.groups()
    else:
        ipstr = urlstr.strip()
        rest = ''
    # Then we try to parse it as an IPv6, and if we fail use
    # QUrl.fromUserInput.
    try:
        ipaddress.IPv6Address(ipstr)
    except ipaddress.AddressValueError:
        return QUrl.fromUserInput(urlstr)
    else:
        return QUrl('http://[{}]{}'.format(ipstr, rest))


def invalid_url_error(url, action):
    """Display an error message for a URL.

    Args:
        action: The action which was interrupted by the error.
    """
    if url.isValid():
        raise ValueError("Calling invalid_url_error with valid URL {}".format(
            url.toDisplayString()))
    errstring = get_errstring(
        url, "Trying to {} with invalid URL".format(action))
    message.error(errstring)


def raise_cmdexc_if_invalid(url):
    """Check if the given QUrl is invalid, and if so, raise a CommandError."""
    if not url.isValid():
        raise cmdutils.CommandError(get_errstring(url))


def get_path_if_valid(pathstr, cwd=None, relative=False, check_exists=False):
    """Check if path is a valid path.

    Args:
        pathstr: The path as string.
        cwd: The current working directory, or None.
        relative: Whether to resolve relative files.
        check_exists: Whether to check if the file
                      actually exists of filesystem.

    Return:
        The path if it is a valid path, None otherwise.
    """
    pathstr = pathstr.strip()
    log.url.debug("Checking if {!r} is a path".format(pathstr))
    expanded = os.path.expanduser(pathstr)

    if os.path.isabs(expanded):
        path = expanded
    elif relative and cwd:
        path = os.path.join(cwd, expanded)
    elif relative:
        try:
            path = os.path.abspath(expanded)
        except OSError:
            path = None
    else:
        path = None

    if check_exists:
        if path is not None:
            try:
                if os.path.exists(path):
                    log.url.debug("URL is a local file")
                else:
                    path = None
            except UnicodeEncodeError:
                log.url.debug(
                    "URL contains characters which are not present in the "
                    "current locale")
                path = None

    return path


def filename_from_url(url):
    """Get a suitable filename from a URL.

    Args:
        url: The URL to parse, as a QUrl.

    Return:
        The suggested filename as a string, or None.
    """
    if not url.isValid():
        return None
    pathname = posixpath.basename(url.path())
    if pathname:
        return pathname
    elif url.host():
        return url.host() + '.html'
    else:
        return None


def host_tuple(url):
    """Get a (scheme, host, port) tuple from a QUrl.

    This is suitable to identify a connection, e.g. for SSL errors.
    """
    if not url.isValid():
        raise InvalidUrlError(url)
    scheme, host, port = url.scheme(), url.host(), url.port()
    assert scheme
    if not host:
        raise ValueError("Got URL {} without host.".format(
            url.toDisplayString()))
    if port == -1:
        port_mapping = {
            'http': 80,
            'https': 443,
            'ftp': 21,
        }
        try:
            port = port_mapping[scheme]
        except KeyError:
            raise ValueError("Got URL {} with unknown port.".format(
                url.toDisplayString()))
    return scheme, host, port


def get_errstring(url, base="Invalid URL"):
    """Get an error string for a URL.

    Args:
        url: The URL as a QUrl.
        base: The base error string.

    Return:
        A new string with url.errorString() is appended if available.
    """
    url_error = url.errorString()
    if url_error:
        return base + " - {}".format(url_error)
    else:
        return base


def same_domain(url1, url2):
    """Check if url1 and url2 belong to the same website.

    This will use a "public suffix list" to determine what a "top level domain"
    is. All further domains are ignored.

    For example example.com and www.example.com are considered the same. but
    example.co.uk and test.co.uk are not.

    Return:
        True if the domains are the same, False otherwise.
    """
    if not url1.isValid():
        raise InvalidUrlError(url1)
    if not url2.isValid():
        raise InvalidUrlError(url2)

    suffix1 = url1.topLevelDomain()
    suffix2 = url2.topLevelDomain()
    if suffix1 == '':
        return url1.host() == url2.host()

    if suffix1 != suffix2:
        return False

    domain1 = url1.host()[:-len(suffix1)].split('.')[-1]
    domain2 = url2.host()[:-len(suffix2)].split('.')[-1]
    return domain1 == domain2


def encoded_url(url):
    """Return the fully encoded url as string.

    Args:
        url: The url to encode as QUrl.
    """
    return bytes(url.toEncoded()).decode('ascii')


class IncDecError(Exception):

    """Exception raised by incdec_number on problems.

    Attributes:
        msg: The error message.
        url: The QUrl which caused the error.
    """

    def __init__(self, msg, url):
        super().__init__(msg)
        self.url = url
        self.msg = msg

    def __str__(self):
        return '{}: {}'.format(self.msg, self.url.toString())


def _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):
    """Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match."""
    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()
    # This should always succeed because we match \d+
    val = int(number)
    if incdec == 'decrement':
        if val < count:
            raise IncDecError("Can't decrement {} by {}!".format(val, count),
                              url)
        val -= count
    elif incdec == 'increment':
        val += count
    else:
        raise ValueError("Invalid value {} for incdec!".format(incdec))
    if zeroes:
        if len(number) < len(str(val)):
            zeroes = zeroes[1:]
        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):
            zeroes += '0'

    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])


# Order of the segments in a URL.
# Each list entry is a tuple of (path name (string), getter, setter).
# Note that the getters must not use FullyDecoded decoded mode to prevent loss
# of information. (host and path use FullyDecoded by default)
_URL_SEGMENTS = [
    (
        'host',
        lambda url: url.host(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),
        lambda url, host: url.setHost(host, QUrl.StrictMode)),
    (
        'port',
        lambda url: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',
        lambda url, x: url.setPort(int(x))),
    (
        'path',
        lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),
        lambda url, path: url.setPath(path, QUrl.StrictMode)),
    (
        'query',
        lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),
        lambda url, query: url.setQuery(query, QUrl.StrictMode)),
    (
        'anchor',
        lambda url: url.fragment(QUrl.PrettyDecoded),
        lambda url, fragment: url.setFragment(fragment, QUrl.StrictMode)),
]


def incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):
    """Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.

    Args:
        url: The current url
        incdec: Either 'increment' or 'decrement'
        count: The number to increment or decrement by
        segments: A set of URL segments to search. Valid segments are:
                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.
                  Default: {'path', 'query'}

    Return:
        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.

    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.
    """
    if not url.isValid():
        raise InvalidUrlError(url)

    if segments is None:
        segments = {'path', 'query'}
    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}
    if segments - valid_segments:
        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments
        raise IncDecError("Invalid segments: {}".format(
            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)

    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original
    url = QUrl(url)
    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards
    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(_URL_SEGMENTS):
        if segment not in segments:
            continue

        # Get the last number in a string not preceded by regex '%' or '%.'
        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\d+)(.*)',
                             getter(url))
        if not match:
            continue

        setter(url, _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))
        return url

    raise IncDecError("No number found in URL!", url)


def file_url(path):
    """Return a file:// url (as string) to the given local path.

    Arguments:
        path: The absolute path to the local file
    """
    return QUrl.fromLocalFile(path).toString(QUrl.FullyEncoded)


def data_url(mimetype, data):
    """Get a data: QUrl for the given data."""
    b64 = base64.b64encode(data).decode('ascii')
    url = QUrl('data:{};base64,{}'.format(mimetype, b64))
    qtutils.ensure_valid(url)
    return url


def safe_display_string(qurl):
    """Get a IDN-homograph phishing safe form of the given QUrl.

    If we're dealing with a Punycode-encoded URL, this prepends the hostname in
    its encoded form, to make sure those URLs are distinguishable.

    See https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/2547
    and https://bugreports.qt.io/browse/QTBUG-60365
    """
    if not qurl.isValid():
        raise InvalidUrlError(qurl)

    host = qurl.host(QUrl.FullyEncoded)
    if '..' in host:  # pragma: no cover
        # WORKAROUND for https://bugreports.qt.io/browse/QTBUG-60364
        return '(unparseable URL!) {}'.format(qurl.toDisplayString())

    for part in host.split('.'):
        if part.startswith('xn--') and host != qurl.host(QUrl.FullyDecoded):
            return '({}) {}'.format(host, qurl.toDisplayString())

    return qurl.toDisplayString()


def query_string(qurl):
    """Get a query string for the given URL.

    This is a WORKAROUND for:
    https://www.riverbankcomputing.com/pipermail/pyqt/2017-November/039702.html
    """
    try:
        return qurl.query()
    except AttributeError:  # pragma: no cover
        return QUrlQuery(qurl).query()


class InvalidProxyTypeError(Exception):

    """Error raised when proxy_from_url gets an unknown proxy type."""

    def __init__(self, typ):
        super().__init__("Invalid proxy type {}!".format(typ))


def proxy_from_url(url):
    """Create a QNetworkProxy from QUrl and a proxy type.

    Args:
        url: URL of a proxy (possibly with credentials).

    Return:
        New QNetworkProxy.
    """
    if not url.isValid():
        raise InvalidUrlError(url)

    scheme = url.scheme()
    if scheme in ['pac+http', 'pac+https', 'pac+file']:
        fetcher = pac.PACFetcher(url)
        fetcher.fetch()
        return fetcher

    types = {
        'http': QNetworkProxy.HttpProxy,
        'socks': QNetworkProxy.Socks5Proxy,
        'socks5': QNetworkProxy.Socks5Proxy,
        'direct': QNetworkProxy.NoProxy,
    }
    if scheme not in types:
        raise InvalidProxyTypeError(scheme)

    proxy = QNetworkProxy(types[scheme], url.host())

    if url.port() != -1:
        proxy.setPort(url.port())
    if url.userName():
        proxy.setUser(url.userName())
    if url.password():
        proxy.setPassword(url.password())
    return proxy

from PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/app')

from qutebrowser.utils.urlutils import incdec_number, IncDecError

# Test 1: Encoded sequence with trailing number
print("Test 1: Encoded sequence with trailing number")
url1 = QUrl("http://localhost/%3A5")
print(f"  Original URL: {url1.toString()}")
try:
    result1 = incdec_number(url1, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})
    print(f"  After increment: {result1.toString()}")
    print(f"  PROBLEM: URL was modified! Expected http://localhost/%3A6")
except IncDecError as e:
    print(f"  Raised error (unexpected): {e.msg}")

# Test 2: Negative numbers after decrement
print("\nTest 2: Negative numbers after decrement")
url2 = QUrl("http://example.com/page_1")
print(f"  Original URL: {url2.toString()}")
try:
    result2 = incdec_number(url2, 'decrement', count=2, segments={'path'})
    print(f"  After decrement by 2: {result2.toString()}")
    print(f"  PROBLEM: Allowed negative number! Expected error")
except IncDecError as e:
    print(f"  Raised error (expected): {e.msg}")

# Test 3: URL-encoded space
print("\nTest 3: URL-encoded space preservation")
url3 = QUrl("http://example.com/%20space/5")
print(f"  Original URL: {url3.toString()}")
try:
    result3 = incdec_number(url3, 'increment', count=1, segments={'path'})
    print(f"  After increment: {result3.toString()}")
    if "%20" in result3.toString():
        print(f"  OK: Encoding preserved")
    else:
        print(f"  PROBLEM: Encoding lost or modified!")
except IncDecError as e:
    print(f"  Raised error: {e.msg}")

# URL Increment/Decrement Regression Test Summary

## Overview
This regression test suite (`regression_test.py`) demonstrates and validates three critical bugs in qutebrowser's URL number increment/decrement feature (`incdec_number` function in `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`).

## Test File Location
- **File**: `/workspace/regression_test.py`
- **Test Classes**: 4 (38 lines per class on average)
- **Total Tests**: 10 (5 passing, 5 failing on buggy code)
- **Runnable with**: `python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py`

## Bugs Demonstrated

### Bug 1: Encoded Sequences with Digits Are Corrupted
**Test**: `TestEncodedSequenceCorruption::test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number`

**Issue**: When a URL contains an encoded digit sequence (e.g., `%35` = encoded '5') followed by an actual digit, the increment/decrement operation corrupts the encoded sequence.

**Example**:
- Input: `http://localhost/%355` (where `%35` = '5', so decoded = `/55`)
- Expected: Preserve the encoding, result should contain `%35`
- Actual: `http://localhost/56` (encoding lost)

**Root Cause**: The code uses `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` to get URL segments, which decodes percent-encoded characters. The regex pattern is then applied to the decoded string, losing information about which digits were originally encoded.

---

### Bug 2: URL-Encoded Data Is Lost/Corrupted
**Tests**: 
- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_space_in_path`
- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_multiple_encoded_sequences`  
- `TestEncodedDataPreservation::test_encoded_unicode_character`
- `TestComplexScenarios::test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space`

**Issue**: URL-encoded characters (spaces, Unicode, special characters) are decoded but when the path is set back using `StrictMode`, it rejects literal spaces and other characters, resulting in invalid URLs.

**Examples**:
1. Input: `http://example.com/my%20file/5` (space encoded as %20)
   - Decoded internally to: `http://example.com/my file/5`
   - After operation: URL becomes invalid (empty string)
   - Expected: `http://example.com/my%20file/6` (encoding preserved)

2. Input: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/5` (encoded Unicode 'ä')
   - Result: `http://example.com/ä/6` (literal character instead of encoding)
   - Expected: `http://example.com/%C3%A4/6` (encoding preserved)

**Root Cause**: The getters use `QUrl.PrettyDecoded`, which decodes certain characters. When the modified string is set back with `QUrl.StrictMode`, it:
- Rejects literal spaces (invalid in URLs)
- Converts Unicode characters to their literal form instead of re-encoding
- Creates invalid or corrupted URLs

---

### Bug 3: Negative Values After Decrement
**Tests**:
- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit`
- `TestNegativeValueHandling::test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative`

**Status**: ✅ PASSING - This bug is NOT present in the current code

**Verification**: The code correctly raises `IncDecError` when attempting to decrement below 0:
```python
if val < count:
    raise IncDecError("Can't decrement {} by {}!".format(val, count), url)
```

---

## Test Results on Buggy Code

```
===== Test Results =====

- test_encoded_colon_with_trailing_number
- test_decrement_below_zero_single_digit
- test_decrement_below_zero_allows_negative
- test_encoded_percent_character
- test_increment_in_query_with_encoded_equals

FAILED:  5 tests
- test_encoded_digit_followed_by_number
  Error: BUG: Encoded sequence %35 was corrupted!
  
- test_encoded_space_in_path
  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')
  
- test_multiple_encoded_sequences
  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')
  
- test_encoded_unicode_character
  Error: BUG: Encoded Unicode %C3%A4 was corrupted!
  
- test_increment_in_anchor_with_encoded_space
  Error: BUG: Result URL became invalid! (returns '')
```

---

## Technical Details

### Problematic Code Section
**File**: `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py` (lines 559-626)

The `_URL_SEGMENTS` tuple (lines 559-580) uses `PrettyDecoded` mode:
```python
_URL_SEGMENTS = [
    ('path', lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),
    ('query', lambda url: url.query(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),
    ...
]
```

This decodes percent-encoded sequences, and the regex pattern:
```python
match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\D|^)(?<!%)(?<!%.)(0*)(\d+)(.*)', getter(url))
```

Cannot properly distinguish between:
- Digits that were originally encoded (e.g., from `%35`)
- Digits that are actual number values to increment

### Why This Is Problematic

1. **Loss of Information**: `PrettyDecoded` removes encoding context needed by the regex
2. **Invalid URL Creation**: `StrictMode` setters reject literal spaces and other characters that were decoded
3. **Regex Ineffectiveness**: The negative lookahead `(?<!%)(?<!%.)` cannot prevent matching digits in encoded sequences because they're already decoded

---

## How to Fix (Design Notes)

The fix would need to:
1. **Preserve Encoding**: Use `QUrl.FullyEncoded` or a mode that preserves percent-encoding
2. **Avoid Decoding**: Apply regex to encoded form, then map matches back to original positions
3. **Safe Re-encoding**: Use appropriate encoding when setting values back
4. **Proper Mode Selection**: Use appropriate QUrl encoding mode when setting segments

---

- **Test File**: `/workspace/regression_test.py`
- **Implementation**: `/app/qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py`
- **Test Framework**: pytest with PyQt5


The tests are self-contained and do not require additional configuration files.

## Root Cause Analysis

**File**: `qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py` (lines 559-626)

The `_URL_SEGMENTS` definition uses `QUrl.PrettyDecoded` mode for getters:
```python
('path', lambda url: url.path(QUrl.PrettyDecoded), ...),
```

This causes:
1. Percent-encoded sequences to be decoded (losing encoding context)
2. The regex to operate on decoded strings where it can't distinguish encoded vs. actual digits
3. The setters with `StrictMode` to reject literal spaces and other characters
4. Result: Invalid or corrupted URLs
